<script type="text/javascript">
    // _gaq = ('_gaq' in window) ? window._gaq : [];
    // window.google_analytics_uacct = 'UA-273774-7';
    try{
        var gatracking = gatracking || {
            parent_selector:'module',
            fire_on_event:'mousedown',
            firing: false,
            initialized: false,
            fire_on:{
                all_events:false,
                engagement:90,
                time:15000,
                errors:true,
                domain:true,
                domReady:false,
                php_time:false,
                islocal:false            },
            uacct:'UA-273774-7',
            elem: {
                is: {
                    eventful:function(obj){
                        var events = obj.data('events');
                        return (events && events !== undefined && events !== null);
                    },
                    actionable: function(obj) {
                        // if attribute is defined use it's value, otherwise assume it's actionable
                        actionable = obj.attr('ga-event-actionable');
                        return (typeof actionable !== 'undefined') ? actionable : true;
                    },
                    submit:function(obj){
                        return (obj.attr('type') !== undefined && obj.attr('type') == "submit");
                    },
                    link:function(obj){
                        return obj.attr('href') !== undefined;
                    },
                    button:function(obj){
                        return obj.is("button");
                    }
                }
            },
            now: function() {
                return ( new Date() ).getTime();
            },
            location:document.location.host.split('.').splice(-2).join('.'),
            initialize:function(options){
                if(this.initialized === true) return false;
                var options = jQuery.extend(gatracking, options),
                    that = this,
                    fallback_time = this.now();

                if (!!'1') {
                    this.set_campaign_params('p_map,null/null/null/null/null/null/30931294,3');
                }

                this.custom_vars();

				this.campaign_tracking();

                this.fire(['_trackPageview']);

                window.google_analytics_uacct = this.uacct;

                if(this.fire_on['errors']){
                    this.trace("Attaching GA error handler");
                    window.onerror = this.error_tracking;
                }
                if(this.fire_on['all_events']){
                    this.trace('Attaching module level event handling');
                    this.eventful_tracking();
                }
                if(this.fire_on['engagement']){
                    this.trace('Attaching engagement event handler');
                    this.engagement_tracking();
                }
                if(this.fire_on['time']){
                    this.trace('Attaching time on site tracking handler');
                    this.time_tracking();
                }
                if(this.fire_on['php_time']){
                    try{
                        var php_time = (end_php_load_time - this.fire_on['php_time']);
                        this.fire(['_trackEvent', 'Performance', 'PHP time', php_time, null, true]);
                    } catch(e) {}
                }
                this.trace('Attaching FB status tracker');
                this.facebook_track();
                if(this.fire_on['domReady']){
                    jQuery(function(){
                        try{
                            var event_time = ( gatracking.now() - (start_cs_load_time || fallback_time) ) / 1000;
                            gatracking.fire(['_trackEvent', 'Performance', 'DOM Ready', event_time, null, true]);
                        }catch(e){}
                    });
                }

                //this tracks all facebox ajax calls
                window.ga_attached = false;
                jQuery('[rel=facebox]').ajaxSuccess(function(e, xhr, options){
                    if(options.dataType !== 'script' && options.dataType !== 'json' && !window.ga_attached){
                        var module = jQuery('#facebox').find('.'+that.parent_selector);
                        that.trace('Attaching async [facebox] listener');
                        that.eventful_tracking(module);
                        window.ga_attached = true;
                        // ajaxSuccess fires multiple times so the ga_attached flag ensures ga event handling is only attached once
                        jQuery(document).bind('close.facebox', function(){
                            window.ga_attached = false;
                        });
                    }
                });
                this.initialized = true;
            },
            custom_vars:function(){
                                    _gaq.push(['_setCustomVar', 1, 'lmi', 'index/article/15509', 3]);

                                    _gaq.push(['_setCustomVar', 42, 'user_new_profile', 'null', 3]);

                            },
            fire:function(params){//fires the google analytics tracking event and traces
                var parameters = params || [];
                if(this.islocal !== true && window['_gaq']){//don't fire tracking events on local requests
                    window['_gaq'].push(parameters);
                }
                this.trace(parameters);
                return this;
            },
            trace:function(params){  },
            eventful_tracking:function(node){

                if(this.firing === false){
                    this.trace('Initializing google analytics tracking');
                    this.firing = true;
                    var target = node || jQuery('.'+this.parent_selector),
                    that = this;

                    if(node && !node.hasClass(this.parent_selector)){
                        return true;
                    }

                    target.delegate('*', that.fire_on_event, function(e){
                        try{

                            var element = jQuery(this),
                                actionable = that.elem.is.actionable(element),
                                tracking_condition = that.elem.is.link(element) || that.elem.is.submit(element) || that.elem.is.button(element) || that.elem.is.eventful(element);

                            if(!tracking_condition && !actionable) {
                                that.trace(element.toString() + ' is not actionable');
                                return true;
                            }

                            var parent = element.closest('.'+that.parent_selector),
                            parent_class = parent.attr('class').replace(that.parent_selector+' ', '').split(' ')[0],
                            parent_full_class = parent_class.replace(/_/g, '/'),
                            module_index = parent.index('.'+parent_class),
                            all_actionable = jQuery('.'+parent_class).actionableItems(),
                            element_index = all_actionable.index(element[0]),
                            params = ['_trackEvent', that.parent_selector, parent_full_class+'_'+module_index, element_index.toString() ];
                            if(that.elem.is.link(element)  && element.attr('href').substring(0) != '#') {
                                that.trace('element is a link');

                                var href = element.attr('href'),
                                domain = href.split('/'),
                                domain_name = domain[2].split('.').splice(-2).join('.');

                                that.trace('Tracking domain name: ' + domain_name);
                                that.trace(href.indexOf(domain_name));
                                if(href.match(/http[s]?\:/) !== null && domain_name.indexOf('answers.com') === -1) {
                                    that.trace('Link is outbound');
                                    that.fire(['_trackEvent', 'Outbound', domain_name, href, null, true]);
                                }
                            }
                            e.stopPropagation();
                            that.fire(params);
                            return true;
                        } catch (e) {
                            that.trace(e + ' in Google Analytics JS');
                            return true;
                        }
                        return true;
                    });
                    this.firing = false;
                }
            },
            facebook_track:function(){
                var fb_event_track = function(){
                    try{
                        FB.getLoginStatus(function(response) {
                            var loggedin_status = false;
                            if (response.status === 'connected' || response.status === 'not_authorized') {
                              loggedin_status = true;
                            }
                            gatracking.fire(['_setCustomVar', 9, 'fb_loggedin', 'fb_loggedin_' + (loggedin_status ? 'yes' : 'no'), 2]);
                            gatracking.fire(['_trackEvent', 'Facebook_' + fb_app_id, 'status', response.status, null, true]);
                            gatracking.fire(['_trackEvent', 'FB_loggedin', 'status', (loggedin_status ? '1' : '0'), null, true]);
                        });
                        FB.Event.subscribe('edge.create', function(href, widget) { gatracking.fire(['_trackSocial', 'Facebook', 'Like', href]); });
                        FB.Event.subscribe('edge.remove', function(href, widget) { gatracking.fire(['_trackSocial', 'Facebook', 'Unlike', href]); });
                        FB.Event.subscribe('message.send', function(href, widget) { gatracking.fire(['_trackSocial', 'Facebook', 'Send', href]); });
                        FB.Event.subscribe('comment.create', function(href, widget) { gatracking.fire(['_trackSocial', 'Facebook', 'Comment', href]); });
                        FB.Event.subscribe('comment.remove', function(href, widget) { gatracking.fire(['_trackSocial', 'Facebook', 'Uncomment', href]); });
                    }catch(e){}
                };

                if(typeof FB !== 'undefined' && FB.Event && FB.Event.subscribe){
                    fb_event_track();
                }
            },
            time_tracking:function(){
                return setTimeout((function(a){
                    var time_on_site = [ parseInt( gatracking.fire_on.time / 1000 ), "seconds on site" ].join(' ');
                    gatracking.fire(['_trackEvent', 'Time', time_on_site, gatracking.fire_on.time.toString(), null, true ]);
                }), gatracking.fire_on.time);
            },
            set_campaign_params: function(campaign_data) {
                var params = {};
                var fields = ['source', 'param4', 'post_id', 'page', 'account_id', 'ad_id', 'article_id'];

                // example campaign_data prior to parse
                // campaign_data = 'p_map,source.2/param4.2/post_id.2/page.2/account_id.2/ad_id.2/article_id.2,3';
                function parse_campaign_data() {
                    try {
                        return campaign_data.split(',')[1].split('/');
                    } catch(e) { return false; }
                }

                campaign_data = parse_campaign_data();

                if (!!campaign_data && !!_gaq) {

                    for (var i = 0; i < fields.length; i++) {
                        params[fields[i]] = campaign_data[i] || '';
                    }

                    this.fire(['_set', 'campaignParams',
                        'utm_campaign=' + params.param4 +
                        '&utm_source='  + 'fb' + // 'always' set to fb if is customvar 35 is present
                        '&utm_medium='  + params.page + '/' + params.account_id +
                        '&utm_content=' + params.article_id + '/' + params.post_id +
                        '&utm_term='    + params.ad_id
                    ]);
                }
            },
            campaign_tracking: function() {

				var campaign_vars = {"camp_name_key":"","camp_source_key":"","camp_medium_key":"","camp_term_key":"","camp_content_key":"","campaign_cookie_timeout":"","campaign_track":""};
				if(campaign_vars.camp_name_key !== "") {
					gatracking.fire(['_setCampNameKey', campaign_vars.camp_name_key]);
				}
				if(campaign_vars.camp_source_key !== "") {
					gatracking.fire(['_setCampSourceKey', campaign_vars.camp_source_key]);
				}
				if(campaign_vars.camp_medium_key !== "") {
					gatracking.fire(['_setCampMediumKey', campaign_vars.camp_medium_key]);
				}
				if(campaign_vars.camp_term_key !== "") {
					gatracking.fire(['_setCampTermKey', campaign_vars.camp_term_key]);
				}
				if(campaign_vars.camp_content_key !== "") {
					gatracking.fire(['_setCampContentKey', campaign_vars.camp_content_key]);
				}
				if(campaign_vars.campaign_cookie_timeout !== "") {
					gatracking.fire(['_setCampaignCookieTimeout', Number(campaign_vars.campaign_cookie_timeout)]);
				}
				if(campaign_vars.campaign_track !== "" && typeof campaign_vars.campaign_track === "boolean") {
					gatracking.fire(['_setCampaignTrack', campaign_vars.campaign_track]);
				}
			},
            error_tracking:function(message, file, line){
                // TODO:  Add error handler for message being an object
                if(typeof message !== "string")
                {
                    return false;
                }

                // Blacklist of errors we don't want to capture
                var blacklist = [
                    'atomicFindClose',  // mysterious mobile Safari error
                    'Script error.',    // same origin browser violation
                    'Can\'t execute code from a freed script'
                ];

                for (i = 0; i < blacklist.length; i++){
                    if (message.indexOf(blacklist[i]) > -1){
                        // Item exists in blacklist, do not send to google
                        return false;
                    }
                }

                var formatted_error_message = '[' + file + ' (' + line + ')] ' + message,
                error_params = ['_trackEvent', 'Exceptions', location.hostname, formatted_error_message, null, true];

                gatracking.fire(error_params);
            },
            engagement_tracking:function() {
                var that = this;
                jQuery(window).scroll(function() {
                    if (typeof window.alreadyScrollTracked != 'undefined')
                        return;

                    var bottom = jQuery(window).height() + jQuery(window).scrollTop(),
                    height = jQuery(document).height(),
                    percentage = Math.round(100*bottom/height);

                    if(percentage > gatracking.fire_on.engagement) {
                        window.alreadyScrollTracked = true;
                        var message = 'Scrolled to ###%'.replace('###', gatracking.fire_on.engagement),
                            scr_params = ['_trackEvent', 'Content Engagement', message, document.location.pathname];
                        that.fire(scr_params);
                    }
                });
            }
        };

        // jQuery(function(){
            if(gatracking.initialized === false){
                gatracking.initialize();
            }
        // });

        jQuery.fn.actionableItems = function(){
            return jQuery(this).find(':actionable') || jQuery([]);
        };

        jQuery.extend(jQuery.expr[':'], {
            actionable:function(element) {
                element = jQuery(element);
                var elem = window.gatracking.elem;
                if( elem.is.eventful(element) || elem.is.submit(element) || elem.is.link(element) ) {
                    return true;
                }
                return false;
            }
        });
    } catch (e) {
        if (window['console'] && console['error']) {
            console.error("gatracking had an error: " + e);
        }
    }

/*
 * Allow GA events via `ga-event` attributes on elements, both those
 * static on the page and those added in dynamically.
 * Elements can have two ga-* related attributes:
 *
 *  - ga-event - ',' separated list of GA _trackEvent parameters
 *  - ga-event-type - {optional} the action that should trigger the event (default is 'click')
 *
 * Elements that have been processed on the page already will have a 'ga-event-added' attribute
 *
 */
$(document).ready(function() {

    // Tracks each ga-event handler, one per event type
    var _handlers = {};


    // Track a 'click' (or other) event on elements with a 'ga-event' attribute
    // The comma separated value of the ga-event attribute follows the params for the _trackEvent()
    // call in google analytics (in same order):
    //
    //  category (required) - name of group wanting to track
    //  action (required) - type of interaction
    //  label (optional) - optional string for identification
    //  value (optional) - numerical data about the event
    //  non-interactive (optional) - true for non-interactive events (ie. it shouldn't be used in bounce-rate calcs)
    //
    // var ga_event_handler = function(ev) {
    var ga_event_handler = function(ev, el) {
        var args = $(el).attr('ga-event').split(/\s*,\s*/),
            len = args.length,
            event = ['_trackEvent'];

        if (length < 2) {
            // throw new Error("[error] [ga-event] attribute tracking missing required arguments on element: %s", this);
            throw new Error("[error] [ga-event] attribute tracking missing required arguments on element: %s", ev.target);
        }

        // build event arguments and push to google analytics
        event = event.concat(args);
        _gaq.push(event);

        // Special handling for 'click's on links
        var href = $(el).attr('href');

        if (ev.type === 'click' && href !== undefined && !/^#/.test(href)) {
            // outbound link, allow ga time to process click event
            ev.preventDefault();
            window.setTimeout(function() {
                window.location.href = href;
            }, 100);
        }
    };


    function poll_ga_attr_events() {
        $('[ga-event]:not([ga-event-added])').each(function() {
            var type = $(this).attr('[ga-event-type]') || 'click',
                selector = '[ga-event][ga-event-added]';

            // Only add a delegated handler once for a given even `type'
            if (!_handlers[type]) {
                // Delegate to handle dynamic elements, track element ref via closure
                $(document).on(type, selector, (function() {
                    return function(ev) {
                        ga_event_handler.apply(null, [ev, ev.currentTarget]);
                    };
                })());
                _handlers[type] = true;
            }

            // mark element as processed
            $(this).attr('ga-event-added', 'true');
        });

        // wait for 100ms and poll again (catch dynmically added elements)
        window.setTimeout(poll_ga_attr_events, 150);
    }


    // let's go, start processing ...
    poll_ga_attr_events();

});

/** Add Post Message Event Listener */
function listen(evnt, elem, func) {
    if (elem.addEventListener) { // W3C DOM
        elem.addEventListener(evnt,func,false);
    }
    else if (elem.attachEvent) { // IE DOM
        var r = elem.attachEvent("on"+evnt, func);
        return r;
    }
}

listen('message', window, function(event){
    if(typeof event !== 'undefined' && typeof event.data === 'String' && event.data.substring(0, 15) == 'DFP Outbound|||')
    {
        var link_data = event.data.split('|||');
        if(link_data.length === 3 && typeof gatracking !== 'undefined')
        {
            gatracking.trace('DFP Link is outbound');
            gatracking.fire(['_trackEvent', link_data[0], link_data[1], link_data[2], null, true]);
        }
    }
});


</script>

</div>

                    <div class="section intro slideshow_flagged  no_image">

                                    
                                                                            <div class="section_body">
                    <p>This odd occurrence has scary movie plot written all over it.</p>                                                                                                </div>
                    </div>

<div class="module subject_section  ">

                    <div class="section paragraph slideshow_flagged ">

                                    
                <span class="section_image"><img class="image" src="//file2.answcdn.com/answ-cld/image/upload/f_jpg,w_672,c_fill,g_faces:center,q_70/v1459176018/visthuwnycfg7gnwheed.jpg" alt="Mowing the lawn is a chore, and unfortunately, the mundane task created more work for homeowners in Aylesbury, England, when THIS happened!"><a href="http://metro.co.uk/2016/03/09/a-massive-hole-with-stairs-has-appeared-in-this-familys-garden-5742692/" target="_blank" class="attribution_link">Masons via Metro</a></span>                                <h2 class="section_title"><span>Mowing the lawn is a chore, and unfortunately, the mundane task created more work for homeowners in Aylesbury, England, when THIS happened!</span></h2>                            <div class="section_body">
                    <p>How in the world did this hole get there? That's exactly what Emma and Kevin James would like to know. Emma was tending to her grass when this portion of her lawn gave way and revealed something incredibly unsettling. This isn't just a small dip in their yard; it's 6.5 feet deep! Although it's difficult to discern in the dark image above, the mysterious pit isn't empty...</p>                                                                                                </div>
                    </div>
                            <div class="section paragraph slideshow_flagged ">

                                    
                <span class="section_image"><img class="image" src="//file2.answcdn.com/answ-cld/image/upload/f_jpg,w_672,c_fill,g_faces:center,q_70/v1459176059/wjqbos3bpth9y23wy0zd.jpg" alt="It contains rusty steps!"><a href="http://metro.co.uk/2016/03/09/a-massive-hole-with-stairs-has-appeared-in-this-familys-garden-5742692/" target="_blank" class="attribution_link">Masons via Metro</a></span>                                <h2 class="section_title"><span>It contains rusty steps!</span></h2>                            <div class="section_body">
                    <p>"It is really odd as there are steps which lead down, but we don't know what to and there was no lid or cover on it," Emma told the&nbsp;<a href="http://metro.co.uk/2016/03/09/a-massive-hole-with-stairs-has-appeared-in-this-familys-garden-5742692/" title="Metro" rel="nofollow" target="_BLANK">Metro</a>. "I don't want to fill it in case there is something historic down there, but it could just be a septic tank or something."&nbsp;<br><br>The 45-year-old teaching assistant has lived on the property for eight years, but it wasn't until November 2015 that she noticed the ground beginning to give way. When she attempted to fix the issue, the area collapsedthankfully not while she nor anyone else was standing on it! In addition to her concern about this particular hole, she's holding her breath that other ditches don't randomly show up in her front yard as well.&nbsp;<br><br>"It was a bit scary and we all jumped back, but when we looked down we couldn't see anything," she explained.&nbsp;<br><br>Fortunately, the pair finally has some peace of mind after the Buckinghamshire County Council contacted them to say they'd solved the nerve-racking mystery!</p>                                                                                                </div>
                    </div>
                            <div class="section paragraph slideshow_flagged ">

                                    
                <span class="section_image"><img class="image" src="//file2.answcdn.com/answ-cld/image/upload/f_jpg,w_672,c_fill,g_faces:center,q_70/v1459176115/icusmimvasatx3hdgalg.jpg" alt="The tunnel is believed to lead to nothing more than a drain."><a href="https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=vXW9BPLC3qw" target="_blank" class="attribution_link">YouTube: Matilda Cross</a></span>                                <h2 class="section_title"><span>The tunnel is believed to lead to nothing more than a drain.</span></h2>                            <div class="section_body">
                    <p>This section of their yard was haphazardly covered more than 30 years earlier, according to a council spokesman. Although it seems their spooky saga will come to a rather anti-climatic close, it will definitely make a great ghost story. Maybe it will inspire the next "Poltergeist" film!</p>                                                                                                </div>
                    </div>
            	

</div>

	<section class="content">
					<div class="image_wrapper" ga-event="Feed_Click,index/article/15509,f_q_8566879" ga-event-added="true">				<a href="http://www.answers.com/Q/How_do_you_mow_the_lawn">					<img src="//file2.answcdn.com/answ-cld/image/upload/w_100,h_100,c_fill,g_face:center,q_60,f_jpg/v1401501397/tgtuo0do35plwffl8jm9.jpg" class="q_image" alt="How do you mow the lawn?" onerror="javascript:this.style.display='none';this.parentNode.parentNode.className = this.parentNode.parentNode.className.replace(/\bsmall_image\b/,'') + ' no_image';this.parentNode.parentNode.parentNode.parentNode.parentNode.className = this.parentNode.parentNode.parentNode.parentNode.parentNode.className.replace(/\bsmall_image\b/,'') + ' no_image'" asg-fluid-img="max">				</a>			</div>				<div class="user_info_text_node contribution" asg-subtext=""><span class="contribution_type"> Answered</span></div>		<div class="category">
			<span asg-subtext="">In</span>				<a class="category_name" href="http://www.answers.com/Q/FAQ/3339">Gardening</a>			</div>						<h1 class="title " ga-event="Feed_Click,index/article/15509,f_q_8566879" ga-event-added="true">
					<a class="title_link black" href="http://www.answers.com/Q/How_do_you_mow_the_lawn">How do you mow the lawn?</a>
				</h1>				<div class="content_text" ga-event="Feed_Click,index/article/15509,f_q_8566879" ga-event-added="true">It depends. The first thing you must do is figure out what type of grass you are mowing. After that you should observe the environmental conditions. If you are mowing turf typ<span class="hellip"></span><span class="hidden">e tall fescue in the Midwest during the spring you'll want to make sure your blades are sharpened and your mowing height is set to 3". Usually one would outline the perimeter of the lawn 2 or 3 times and then work back and forth from one side of the lawn to the other. Be sure to clean your mower when you're done, and don't forget to disconnect the spark plug wire when doing so. </span>				<a href="http://www.answers.com/Q/How_do_you_mow_the_lawn" class="continue_reading">(MORE)</a>		</div>

						var fbappinit = (function() {
							var container = document.getElementById('fbappinit_plugin');
							var app_queue = {"ids":[7080074318,20738101946,106548749379931,117024141736935,124318160942877,125363437505916,131401703561418,133451120007663,137767829572142,145777408819173,160971530656135,193466177382032]};

							function addIframe(app_id) {
								var src = "/solo/social/fbappinit/initjs?app_id="+app_id;
								var iframe = document.createElement('iframe');
								iframe.src = src;
								iframe.style.display = "none";
								container.appendChild(iframe);
							}

							//cross browswer way to add event listener
							function addEvent(element, evnt, funct){
								if (element.attachEvent) {
									return element.attachEvent("on"+evnt, funct);
								} else if (element.addEventListener) {
									return element.addEventListener(evnt, funct, false);
								}
							}

							return {
								init : function () {
									//add iframe(s) to page after everything else has loaded
									addEvent(window, "load", this.authAttempt);
								},

								authAttempt : function () {
									//console.log("auth attempt");
									//console.log(app_queue);
									if (app_queue.ids && app_queue.ids.length > 0) {
										var app_id = app_queue.ids.pop();
										if (app_id) {
											addIframe(app_id);
										}
									}
								}
							}
						})();
